**（100學年度入學新生適用）**

colspan="9"><ol><li>有關共同必修及通識教育科目之詳細規定，另依據「元智大學共同必修科目表」之規定辦理。</li><li>括弧內數字為學分數。</li><li>必修科目計：111學分，專業選修科目至少需選修本系選修科目表課程共計15學分（工程學院其他系所選修課程至多可採計6學分為系選修；外籍生選修工程學院之系所課程得採計為系選修），始能符合畢業學分數。</li><li>最低畢業學分：<strong>130</strong>學分。</li><li>實驗課程需5選3。【實驗(一)：材料與固力(ME348)；實驗(二)：流力與熱傳(ME349)；實驗(三)：生醫機械系統(ME350)；實驗(四)：量測與儀器(ME351)；實驗(五)：綠色能源(ME352)】。</li><li>2選1必修：近代生物學導論(ME114)、工業應用化學(ME229)。</li><li>專業實習課程需3選1。【暑期專業實習(ME477, 0)、學士論文(ME479, 0)、半年專業實習(ME453, 6)，不限年級皆可修課】。</li><li>應用力學-靜力(ME108)未達60分則擋修應用力學-動力(ME214)。</li><li><strong>三年級下學期「機械設計」(ME301)為本系終端學習課程。</strong></li></ol></td></tr></table>

AA-CP-04-CF02 (1.3版)／102.01.21修訂

credits.</li><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>The maximum credits for general education courses are 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>本系同學總共必須修滿130學分方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共31學分、本系必修77學分，其餘選修22學分（外系選修至多承認17學分）。</li></ol><p>Student must take 130 credits in total for graduation, include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (31), Department Required courses (74), and Elective courses (22). (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the 17 credits)</p><ol><li>實驗課程需5選3。【實驗(一)：材料與固力(ME348)；實驗(二)：流力與熱傳(ME349)；實驗(三)：生醫機械系統(ME350)；實驗(四)：量測與儀器(ME351)；實驗(五)：綠色能源(ME352)】。</li></ol><p>Experiments from (I) to (V), please at least choose three out of the five courses. (Exp (I) : Materials and Solid Mechanics ME348(1)；Exp (II) : Fluid Mechanics and Heat Transfer ME349(1)；Exp (III) : Biomechanical Systems ME350(1)；Exp (IV) : Measurement and Instrumentation ME351(1)；Exp (V) : Green Energy ME352(1) ).</p><ol><li>2選1必修：近代生物學導論(ME114)、工業應用化學(ME229)。</li></ol><p>For two courses of “Introduction to Modern Biology ME114(3)” and “Applied Chemistry in Industry ME229(3)”, please choose one course for the required courses credits.</p><ol><li>暑期專業實習(ME477, 0)、學士論文(ME479, 0)及半年專業實習(ME453, 6)課程需3選1，不限年級皆可修課。各課程修課規定請參閱機械工程學系專業實習及學士論文課程修課辦法。</li></ol><p>For these courses of “Summer Internship ME477(0) ”; “Bachelor Thesis ME479(0)” and “Advanced Field Study ME453(6)”, please choose one of the three courses for the required course credits. It’s not required for a grade. Please refer to the methodology of Professional Internships and Bachelor Thesis Courses in the Department of Mechanical Engineering.</p><ol><li>應用力學-靜力(ME108)未達60分則擋修應用力學-動力(ME214)。</li></ol><p>For “Applied Mechanics Statics ME108(3)”, if your scores is less than 60 points, you are not allowed to register “Applied Mechanics Dynamics ME214(3)”.</p><ol><li>本系必修課程初次修課須在本系修讀始予承認。</li></ol><p>The first compulsory courses have to be taken in department of Mechanical Engineering.</p><ol><li>三年級下學期「機械設計」(ME301)為本系終端學習課程。</li></ol><p>Mechanical Design ME301(3) is a experiential learning course.</p><ol><li>「議題導向實作專題課程」必修3學分(需7選1)【機械系統分析(ME386)、綠色能源專題實作(ME387)、機電整合(ME411)、可程式控制(ME415)、自動化機械設計(ME441)、專利分析(ME478)及創新產品設計(ME610)】</li></ol><p>Analysis of Mechanical System ME386(3), Projects for Green Energy ME387(3), Mechatronics Integration ME411(3), Sequential Programmable Control ME415(3), Machine Design Practice ME441(3), Patent Analysis ME478(3), Innovative Product Design ME610(3) are courses of 'Topic and Implementation-oriented courses'. **Department of Mechanical Engineering, Yuan Ze University**

For those who would like to registered “Fundamental computer programming”, he/she has to meet the college requirement. (Course Name: Fundamental Computer Programming)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="17"><p>外語課程應依「通識外語修課規定」修習，共計10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，應修習主題式英語課程三學期5學分，畢業前需修畢三個不同英語課程，始取得畢業資格。大一英語能力後測TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」，修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注事意項，請參照「英語檢定」修課規定。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生(不含交換生)修習「華語一」或「華語二」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語三」、「華語四」、「華語五」、「華語六」，若修習「華語三」、「華語四」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語五」或「華語檢定」。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses as follows:</p><ul><li>English (I), (II): 4 credits</li><li>English thematic course: 5 credits </li><li>English Test: 1 credit</li></ul><p>English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence-based to complete within two semesters.</p><p>English thematic courses are 5-credit of English courses; students are required to obtain </p><p>5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation.</p><p>For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students, exchange students excluded, must score 60 points or higher to pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III), (IV), (V), and (VI). Students must score 60 points or higher in Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and (VI).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing(1)、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books(2)、服務學習Service Learning(1)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="5"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="17"><p>體育除修習大一至大二4個學期外，另需通過「游泳能力檢定」及「心肺適能檢定」等二項檢測，列為畢業門檻。</p><p>Beside taking PE courses for 4 semesters (Year 1 to 2), students must pass both swimming and cardiopulmonary function tests.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education </p><p>(10)</p></td><td colspan="17"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary and General Education courses (31), Department Required courses (74), and Elective courses (22). (Exp (I) : Materials and Solid Mechanics ME348(1)；Exp (II) : Fluid Mechanics and Heat Transfer ME349(1)；Exp (III) : Biomechanical Systems ME350(1)；Exp (IV) : Measurement and Instrumentation ME351(1)；Exp (V) : Green Energy ME352(1) ).</p><ol><li>2選1必修：近代生物學導論(ME114)、工業應用化學(ME229)。</li></ol><p>For two courses of “Introduction to Modern Biology ME114(3)” and “Applied Chemistry in Industry ME229(3)”, please choose one course for the required courses credits.</p><ol><li>暑期專業實習(ME477, 0)、學士論文(ME479, 0)及半年專業實習(ME453, 6)課程需3選1，不限年級皆可修課。各課程修課規定請參閱機械工程學系專業實習及學士論文課程修課辦法。</li></ol><p>For these courses of “Summer Internship ME477(0) ”; “Bachelor Thesis ME479(0)” and “Advanced Field Study ME453(6)”, please choose one of the three courses for the required course credits. It’s not required for a grade. Please refer to the methodology of Professional Internships and Bachelor Thesis Courses in the Department of Mechanical Engineering.</p><ol><li>本系必修課程初次修課須在本系修讀始予承認。</li></ol><p>The first compulsory courses have to be taken in department of Mechanical Engineering.</p><ol><li>三年級下學期「機械設計」(ME301)為本系終端學習課程。</li></ol><p>Mechanical Design ME301(3) is a experiential learning course.</p><ol><li>「議題導向實作專題課程」必修3學分(需7選1)【機械系統分析(ME386)、綠色能源專題實作(ME387)、機電整合(ME411)、可程式控制(ME415)、自動化機械設計(ME441)、專利分析(ME478)及創新產品設計(ME610)】</li></ol><p>Analysis of Mechanical System ME386(3), Projects for Green Energy ME387(3), Mechatronics Integration ME411(3), Sequential Programmable Control ME415(3), Machine Design Practice ME441(3), Patent Analysis ME478(3), Innovative Product Design ME610(3) are courses of 'Topic and Implementation-oriented courses'. Please choose one course for the required course credits.</p><ol><li>「數位應用相關課程｣包括：機械畫(ME475)、電腦輔助分析(ME318)、電腦機械繪圖(ME444)、數值分析(ME345)、應力分析實務(ME476)、有限元素法(ME517)及電腦輔助實務分析與應用(ME522)，畢業前須修習至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Mechanical Drawing ME475(2)<strong>, </strong>Computer-Aided Engineering Analysis ME318(3), Computer-Aided Drafting ME444(3), Numerical Analysis ME345 (3)<strong> ,</strong> Practice of Stress Analysis ME476(3)<strong> ,</strong> Finite Element Method ME517(3)<strong> ,</strong> Computer Aided Analysis for Mechanical Design ME522(3) are courses of 'digital application courses'.  Students are required to take at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p></td></tr></table>

(Exp (I) : Materials and Solid Mechanics ME348(1)；Exp (II) : Fluid Mechanics and Heat Transfer ME349(1)；Exp (III) : Biomechanical Systems ME350(1)；Exp (IV) : Measurement and Instrumentation ME351(1)；Exp (V) : Green Energy ME352(1) ).</s></p><ol><li><s>2選1必修：近代生物學導論(ME114)、工業應用化學(ME229)。</s></li></ol><p><s>For two courses of “Introduction to Modern Biology ME114(3)” and “Applied Chemistry in Industry ME229(3)”, please choose one course for the required courses credits.</s></p><ol><li><s>暑期專業實習(ME477, 0)、學士論文(ME479, 0)及半年專業實習(ME453, 6)課程需3選1，不限年級皆可修課。各課程修課規定請參閱機械工程學系專業實習及學士論文課程修課辦法。</s></li></ol><p><s>For these courses of “Summer Internship ME477(0) ”; “Bachelor Thesis ME479(0)” and “Advanced Field Study ME453(6)”, please choose one of the three courses for the required course credits. It’s not required for a grade. Please refer to the methodology of Professional Internships and Bachelor Thesis Courses in the Department of Mechanical Engineering.</s></p><ol><li>本系必修課程初次修課須在本系修讀始予承認。</li></ol><p>The first compulsory courses have to be taken in department of Mechanical Engineering.</p><ol><li>三年級下學期「機械設計(二)」(ME310)為本系終端學習課程。</li></ol><p>Mechanical Design (II) ME310 (3) is an experiential learning course.</p><ol><li>「ME306機械設計(一)」課程為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分。</li></ol><p>「ME306 Mechanical Design (I) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses"</p><p><s>「議題導向實作專題課程」必修3學分(需7選1)【機械系統分析(ME386)、綠色能源專題實作(ME387)、機電整合(ME411)、可程式控制(ME415)、自動化機械設計(ME441)、專利分析(ME478)及創新產品設計(ME610)】</s></p><p><s>Analysis of Mechanical System ME386(3), Projects for Green Energy ME387(3), Mechatronics Integration ME411(3), Sequential Programmable Control ME415(3), Machine Design Practice ME441(3), Patent Analysis ME478(3), Innovative Product Design ME610(3) are courses of 'Topic and Implementation-oriented courses'. Please choose one course for the required course credits.</s></p><ol><li>「數位應用相關課程｣包括：機械畫(ME475)、電腦輔助分析(ME318)、電腦機械繪圖(ME444)、數值分析(ME345)、應力分析實務(ME476)、有限元素法(ME517)及電腦輔助實務分析與應用(ME522)，畢業前須修習至少2門「數位應用相關課程」(可至本系或外系修習)。</li></ol><p>Mechanical Drawing ME475(2)<strong>, </strong>Computer-Aided Engineering Analysis ME318(3), Computer-Aided Drafting ME444(3), Numerical Analysis ME345 (3)<strong>,</strong> Practice of Stress Analysis ME476(3)<strong>,</strong> Finite Element Method ME517(3)<strong> ,</strong> Computer Aided Analysis for Mechanical Design ME522(3) are courses of 'digital application courses'.  Students are required to take at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including  English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p></td></tr></table>

(Course Name: Fundamental Computer Programming)</p></td></tr><tr><td colspan="16"><p>外語課程應修習10學分。</p><ol><li>「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」為基礎課程，採能力分級上課，共計二學期四學分。</li><li>除了「英語（一）」及「英語（二）」外，畢業前應修畢三個不同主題式英語課程，共三學期5學分。</li><li>大一英語能力後測「TOEIC模擬測驗」成績未達350分者，應修習「應試加強班」(EL260)。修習「應試加強班」期間之期末TOEIC模擬測驗成績未達350分者，則該科成績將「不及格」，並應再次修習「應試加強班」，直到取得TOEIC模擬測驗分數達350分(含)始得修習其他主題式英語課程。</li><li>另開設「英語檢定」(EL360)計一學期1學分，「英語檢定」之修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」，並由通識教學部公佈後施行。</li></ol><p>外國學生改修華語須經國際語言文化中心審核通過始可改修華語課程10學分，其華語課程10學分應含「華語檢定」1學分，「華語檢定」修課限制與注意事項，請參照「通識外語『英語檢定』修課規定」。</p><p>凡本校大學部外國學生修習「華語(一)」或「華語(二)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」。若修習「華語(三)」、「華語(四)」任一課程成績未達60分，不得修習「華語(五)」或「華語檢定」(EL372)。</p><p>The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><ol><li>English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credit elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 5 credits: English thematic courses are 5-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 5 credits through 3 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take “English Testing” (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points in TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” (EL360) for the total 1 credit: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to "the Regulation for Registering English Test" announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li></ol><p>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English.</p><p>The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking Mandarin Chinese (V) and Chinese Proficiency Test (EL372).</p><p>英語檢定English Testing (1)、經典五十Fifty Canonized Books(2)、服務學習Service Learning (1)</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education(0)</p></td><td><p>體育</p><p>Physical Education(0)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education(0)</p></td><td colspan="4"><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education</p><p>(0)</p></td><td></td><td colspan="3"></td><td colspan="2"></td><td colspan="2"></td></tr><tr><td colspan="16"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education </p><p>(10)</p></td><td colspan="16"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生可於四大領域中選課。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. (Exp (I) : Materials and Solid Mechanics ME348(1)；Exp (II) : Fluid Mechanics and Heat Transfer ME349(1)；Exp (III) : Biomechanical Systems ME350(1)；Exp (IV) : Measurement and Instrumentation ME351(1)；Exp (V) : Green Energy ME352(1) ).</s></p><ol><li><s>2選1必修：近代生物學導論(ME114)、工業應用化學(ME229)。</s></li></ol><p><s>For two courses of “Introduction to Modern Biology ME114(3)” and “Applied Chemistry in Industry ME229(3)”, please choose one course for the required courses credits.</s></p><ol><li><s>暑期專業實習(ME477, 0)、學士論文(ME479, 0)及半年專業實習(ME453, 6)課程需3選1，不限年級皆可修課。各課程修課規定請參閱機械工程學系專業實習及學士論文課程修課辦法。</s></li></ol><p><s>For these courses of “Summer Internship ME477(0) ”; “Bachelor Thesis ME479(0)” and “Advanced Field Study ME453(6)”, please choose one of the three courses for the required course credits. It’s not required for a grade. Please refer to the methodology of Professional Internships and Bachelor Thesis Courses in the Department of Mechanical Engineering.</s></p><ol><li>本系必修課程初次修課須在本系修讀始予承認。</li></ol><p>The first compulsory courses have to be taken in department of Mechanical Engineering.</p><ol><li>三年級下學期「機械設計(二)」(ME310)為本系終端學習課程。</li></ol><p>Mechanical Design (II) ME310 (3) is a experiential learning course.</p><ol><li>「ME306機械設計(一)」課程為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分。</li></ol><p>「ME306 Mechanical Design (I) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses"</p><p><s>「議題導向實作專題課程」：必修3學分(需7選1)【本系開設之課程包括機械系統分析(ME386)、綠色能源專題實作(ME387)、機電整合(ME411)、可程式控制(ME415)、自動化機械設計(ME441)、專利分析(ME478)及創新產品設計(ME610)】</s></p><p><s>Analysis of Mechanical System ME386(3), Projects for Green Energy ME387(3), Mechatronics Integration ME411(3), Sequential Programmable Control ME415(3), Machine Design Practice ME441(3), Patent Analysis ME478(3), Innovative Product Design ME610(3) are courses of 'Topic and Implementation-oriented courses'. Please choose one course for the required course credits.</s></p><ol><li>「數位應用相關課程｣：畢業前須於本系或至外系修習至少2門數位應用相關課程【本系開設之課程包括機械畫(ME475)、電腦輔助分析(ME318)、電腦機械繪圖(ME444)、數值分析(ME345)、應力分析實務(ME476)、有限元素(ME517)、電腦輔助實務分析與應用(ME522) 】</li></ol><p>Mechanical Drawing ME475(2)<strong>, </strong>Computer-Aided Engineering Analysis ME318(3), Computer-Aided Drafting ME444(3), Numerical Analysis ME345(3)<strong>,</strong> Practice of Stress Analysis ME476(3)<strong>,</strong> Finite Element Method ME517(3)<strong>,</strong> Computer Aided Analysis for Mechanical Design ME522(3) are courses of 'digital application courses'.  Students are required to take at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程(含英專班)，其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’ English, we encourage students to take the courses in English (including  English Bachelor), which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><ol><li><strong>畢業前至少須完成以下其中一項。</strong></li></ol><p><strong>Before graduation, students must complete at least one of the following. </strong></p><ol><li><strong>專業實習（校外）課程：半年專業實習(ME453、6學分)。</strong></li></ol><p><strong>Professional Internship Course (off-campus): Advanced Field Study ME453(6).</strong></p><ol><li><strong>專題製作（校內）課程：專題研究（一）(ME311、1學分)。</strong></li></ol><p><strong>Project Course (on-campus): Research Project (I) ME311(1).</strong></p><ol><li><strong>海外研習。<br/>Overseas Study.</strong></li></ol></td></tr></table>

（II） for the total 4 credits: English （I） and （II） are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing （EL260） course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </li><li>“English Testing” （EL160） is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</li><li>Foreign students need approval by ILCC for taking 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. Students are required to take at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程（含英專班），其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’English, we encourage students to take the courses in English（including English Bachelor）, which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><ol><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li></ol><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><ol><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p><ol><li><strong>畢業前至少須完成以下其中一項。</strong></li></ol><p><strong>Before graduation, students must complete at least one of the following.</strong></p><ol><li><strong>專業實習（校外）課程：半年專業實習(ME453、6學分)。</strong></li></ol><p><strong>Professional Internship Course (off-campus): Advanced Field Study ME453(6).</strong></p><ol><li><strong>專題製作（校內）課程：專題研究（一）(ME311、1學分)。</strong></li></ol><p><strong>Project Course (on-campus): Research Project (I) ME311(1).</strong></p><ol><li><strong>海外研習。<br/>Overseas Study.</strong></li></ol></td></tr></table>

The undergraduate students must complete 10 required credits of foreign language courses.</p><p>2.	English (I) &amp; (II) for the total 4 credits: English (I) and (II) are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</p><p>3.	English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </p><p>4.	Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing (EL260) course. Students will fail the course if they do not score higher than 350 points of TOEIC Mock Exam by the end of the course, and must repeatedly take the course until they can score higher than 350 points. </p><p>5.	“English Testing” (EL160) is a 2-credit course: For the requirements of registering “English Testing”, please refer to The Regulation for Registering English Test announced and implemented by the College of General Education.</p><p>6.	Foreign students could take 10 credits of Mandarin Chinese courses as alternative courses of English. The 10 credits in Mandarin Chinese courses must include 2 credits for “Chinese Proficiency Test”. For the specific restrictions and considerations for taking the “Chinese Proficiency Test”, please refer to the 'General Education Foreign Language “English Proficiency Exam” Course Requirements' and 'Yuan Ze University Regulations for Exempting the Mandarin Chinese as a Foreign Language Credit ' for more details.</p><p>7. The undergraduate foreign students must pass Mandarin Chinese (I) and (II) before taking Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV). Students must pass Mandarin Chinese (III) and (IV) before taking 'Chinese Proficiency Test' (EL375).</p><p> 英語檢定English Testing（2）、經典選讀A Guide to Classics（2）、服務學習Service Learning（1） </p></td></tr><tr><td><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>體育Physical Education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td><p>興趣選項體育optional physical education（0）</p></td><td></td><td></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td colspan="9"><p>大學部必須修習4學期體育課程；其中2學期為大一體育課程原班級上課，另2學期為興趣選項體育課程。</p><p>The undergraduate students must attend the physical education course for 4 semesters; 2 semesters for the freshman physical education courses, the other two semesters for the optional physical education courses.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>通識教育科目</p><p>General Education（10）</p></td><td colspan="9"><p>通識課程分為人文藝術、自然科學、社會科學及生命科學四大類。學生須於四大領域中各選修2學分課程，共計8學分。General Education program comprises four categories：Humanities, Natural Science, Social Science and Life Science. Students are required to take a 2-credit course from each category to get 8 credits before graduation.</p><p>通識跨域課程General Education Interdisciplinary Course：此2學分學生可自由於通識講座課程、微課自主學習或在地多元文化課群中選課。惟外籍生仍須於四大領域中選課。Students can select the 2 credits from a General Education Lecture course, Micro Credit courses, Self-Study courses, or Local-Multicultural courses. Only foreign students are required to take a 2-credit course from the four categories.</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>院必修科目</p><p>College</p><p>Compulsory</p><p>（4）</p></td><td colspan="9"><p>程式語言共4學分，依各院修課規則辦理。</p><p>The Fundamental Computer Programming has 4 credits in total, which is subject to the rules of each college.</p></td></tr><tr><td rowspan="5"><p>系必修科目Department Compulsory</p><p> （65）</p></td><td><p>微積分(一)</p><p>Calculus (I)</p><p>ME105(3)</p></td><td><p>微積分(二)</p><p>Calculus (II)</p><p>ME107(3)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>工程數學(一)</p><p>Engineering Mathematics (I)</p><p>ME202(3)</p></td><td><p>工程數學(二)</p><p>Engineering Mathematics (II)</p><p>ME204(3)</p></td><td><p>機械設計(一)</p><p>Mechanical Design (I)</p><p>ME306(3)</p></td><td><p>機械設計(二)</p><p>Mechanical Design (II)</p><p>ME310(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>工程圖學</p><p>Engineering Drawing</p><p>ME119(2)</p></td><td><p>工程材料</p><p>Engineering Materials</p><p>ME115(3)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>熱力學(一)</p><p>Thermodynamics (I)</p><p>ME206(3)</p></td><td><p>機動學</p><p>Mechanisms</p><p>ME207(3)</p></td><td><p>流體力學</p><p>Fluid Mechanics</p><p>ME305(3)</p></td><td><p>熱傳學</p><p>Heat Transfer</p><p>ME322(3)</p></td><td></td><td></td></tr><tr><td><p>機械工程概論</p><p>Introduction to Mechanical Engineering</p><p>ME127(1)</p></td><td><p>普通物理</p><p>General Physics</p><p>ME117(3)</p></td><td colspan="2"><p>應用力學-動力</p><p>Applied Mechanics Dynamics</p><p>ME214(3)</p></td><td><p>材料力學</p><p>Mechanics of Materials</p><p>ME309(3)</p></td><td><p>機械工程實驗 (一)</p><p>Mechanical Engineering Lab.(I)</p><p>ME307(1)</p></td><td><p>機械工程實驗(二)</p><p>Mechanical Engineering Lab. regulations.</p><ol><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the exceeding credits will not be counted.</p><ol><li>終端學習課程：「機械設計(二) (ME310)」</li></ol><p>The experiential learning courses：Mechanical Design (II) ME310(3).</p><ol><li>「機械設計(一) (ME306)」為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分. </li></ol><p>Mechanical Design (I) ME306(3) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses".</p><ol><li>「數位應用相關課程｣：畢業前須通過至少2門數位應用相關課程（可至本系或外系修習）【本系開設之課程包括機械畫(ME475)、電腦輔助分析(ME318)、電腦機械繪圖(ME444)、數值分析(ME345)、應力分析實務(ME476)】。</li></ol><p>    Mechanical Drawing ME475(2)<strong>, </strong>Computer-Aided Engineering Analysis ME318(3), Computer-Aided Drafting ME444(3), Numerical Analysis ME345(3)<strong>,</strong> Practice of Stress Analysis ME476(3)<strong>,</strong> are courses of 'digital application courses'.  Students are required to take at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>本系同學總共必須修滿 128學分及<strong>完成任一個跨領域學程</strong>方可畢業，包括共同必修及通識課程共27學分、院必修程式語言課程共4學分、本系必修65學分，選修32學分【自由選修至多承認17學分(含專業自主學習至多3學分)。與他系合作之學程，依學程規定承認最高學分】。</li></ol><p>Student of Dept. of ME must take 128 credits in total for graduation and complete one of the Interdisciplinary Curricula for graduation, include Required Common Courses and General Education courses (27) credits, College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming (4) credits, Department Compulsory courses (65） credits, and Department Elective courses (32) credits. (A maximum of (17) credits can be recognized for free electives, including up to 3 credits for Disciplinary self-directed learning. For the cooperation courses with other departments, credits will be recognized according to the specific program regulations.）</p><ol><li>本系必修課程初次修課須在本系修讀始予承認。</li></ol><p>The first compulsory courses have to be taken in department of Mechanical Engineering.</p><ol><li><a></a>畢業前至少須完成以下其中一項。</li></ol><p>Before graduation, students must complete at least one of the following.</p><ol><li>專業實習（校外）課程：半年專業實習(ME453、6學分)。</li></ol><p>Professional Internship Course (off-campus): Advanced Field Study ME453(6).</p><ol><li>專題製作（校內）課程：專題研究（一）(ME311、1學分)。</li></ol><p>Project Course (on-campus): Research Project (I) ME311(1).</p><ol><li>海外研習。</li></ol><p>Overseas Study.</p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程（含英專班），其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’English, we encourage students to take the courses in English（including English Bachelor）, which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><ol><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li></ol><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><ol><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p></td></tr></table>

（II） for the total 4 credits: English （I） and （II） are 4 credits elementary courses for the freshmen who are grouped on English competence; to complete within two semesters.</li><li>English thematic course for the total 4 credits: English thematic courses are 4-credit English courses; students are required to obtain 4 credits through 2 different thematic courses for graduation. </li><li>Students who do not reach the 350-point threshold of TOEIC Mock Exam in the end of the freshman year must take English Testing （EL260） course. Common Required Course List for General Education courses information and regulations.</p><ol><li>通識教育科目學分只採計至多10學分，超修之學分將不列入畢業學分。</li></ol><p>The maximum credits for general education courses is 10, the Interdisciplinary Curricula for graduation, include Required Common Courses and General Education courses（27）credits, College Compulsory Courses Fundamental Computer Programming（4）credits, Department Compulsory courses（62）credits, and Department Elective courses（35）credits. (Outside the Department of elective up to recognize the （17）credits, and the cooperation courses with other departments, according to the provisions of the highest recognition of credit）</p><ol><li>本系必修課程初次修課須在本系修讀始予承認。</li></ol><p>The first compulsory courses have to be taken in department of Mechanical Engineering.</p><ol><li>三年級下學期「機械設計(二)」(ME310)為本系終端學習課程。</li></ol><p>Mechanical Design (II) ME310(3) is an experiential learning course.</p><ol><li>「ME306機械設計(一)」課程為本系必修「議題導向實作專題課程」3學分。</li></ol><p>「ME306 Mechanical Design (I) is a compulsory three-credit course of "Topic and Implementation-oriented courses"</p><ol><li>「數位應用相關課程｣：畢業前須於本系或至外系修習至少2門數位應用相關課程【本系開設之課程包括機械畫(ME475)、電腦輔助分析(ME318)、電腦機械繪圖(ME444)、數值分析(ME345)、應力分析實務(ME476)】</li></ol><p>Mechanical Drawing ME475(2)<strong>, </strong>Computer-Aided Engineering Analysis ME318(3), Computer-Aided Drafting ME444(3), Numerical Analysis ME345 (3)<strong> ,</strong> Practice of Stress Analysis ME476(3)<strong> ,</strong> are courses of 'digital application courses'.  Students are required to take at least two 'digital application courses'. (Student may take 'digital application courses' from another department.)</p><ol><li>為增進學生英文能力，鼓勵選修英語授課課程（含英專班），其修習之課程科目及學分數之認抵需依學系規定辦理。</li></ol><p>To improve students’English, we encourage students to take the courses in English（including English Bachelor）, which courses and credits waiver and transference should be standardized by each department.</p><ol><li>自106學年度起軍訓課程由必修改為選修，該學分納入當學期修課學分數計算，但不納入畢業總學分計算。</li></ol><p>The military education courses are no longer compulsory starting the 106 academic year. The military education courses will not be accumulated to the graduation requirements, but they can be counted as taken credits for each semester.</p><ol><li>修習碩士班課程以大三以上學生為限，且不得修習碩士在職專班課程。</li></ol><p>Master's degree courses are limited to students in their third year or above, and students are not allowed to take courses from the Executive Master program.</p><ol><li><strong>畢業前至少須完成以下其中一項。</strong></li></ol><p><strong>Before graduation, students must complete at least one of the following.</strong></p><ol><li><strong>專業實習（校外）課程：半年專業實習(ME453、6學分)。</strong></li></ol><p><strong>Professional Internship Course (off-campus): Advanced Field Study ME453(6).</strong></p><ol><li><strong>專題製作（校內）課程：專題研究（一）(ME311、1學分)。</strong></li></ol><p><strong>Project Course (on-campus): Research Project (I) ME311(1).</strong></p><ol><li><strong>海外研習。<br/>Overseas Study.</strong></li></ol></td></tr></table>

**元智大學機械工程學系輔系科目表 (111學年度適用)**

**List of Minor Courses for the Department of Mechanical Engineering of Yuan Ze University**

**（Applicable to Students Admitted for Academic year of 2022-2023）**

111.04.20 一一○學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2021, on April 20, 2022

<table><thead><tr><th><p>輔系名稱</p><p>Department</p></th><th><p>輔系科目</p><p>Minor Courses</p></th><th><p>學分數</p><p>Credits</p></th><th><p>備註</p><p>Remarks</p></th></tr></thead><tbody><tr><td rowspan="18"><p>機械工程學系</p><p>Department of Mechanical Engineering</p></td><td><p>應用力學-靜力</p><p>Applied Mechanics Statics</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td rowspan="7"><p>必修</p><p>Required Courses</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>應用力學-動力</p><p>Applied Mechanics Dynamics</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>機動學</p><p>Mechanisms</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>熱力學（上）</p><p>Thermo-dynamics (I)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>機械設計（上）</p><p>Mechanical Design(I)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>流體力學</p><p>Fluid Mechanics</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>共計</p><p>Total</p></td><td><p>18</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>工程材料</p><p>Engineering Materials</p></td><td><p>3</p></td><td rowspan="11"><p>選修</p><p>Elective Courses（至少需修滿12學分（含）以上</p><p>At least take 12 credits above）</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>熱力學（下）<br/>Thermo-dynamics (II)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>材料力學</p><p>Mechanics of Material</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>機械設計（下）</p><p>Mechanical Design(II)</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>工程圖學</p><p>Engineering Graphics</p></td><td><p>2</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>自動控制</p><p>Automatic Control</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>機械製造</p><p>Introduction to Manufacturing Processes</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>機械畫</p><p>Mechanical Drawing</p></td><td><p>2</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>電路及電子學</p><p>Introduction to Electric Circuits and Electronics</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>數值分析</p><p>Numerical Analysis</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>共計</p><p>Total</p></td><td><p>28</p></td></tr></tbody></table>

註：本系輔系最低須修滿30學分，且每科皆需達到60分以上。

P.S.: Must earn at least 30 credits for Minor Courses of ME department and each course needs more than 60 points
```

colspan="4"><ol><li>最低畢業學分數：30學分（包含6學分論文）。</li><li>必修科目：書報討論（0學分）需於兩年內修完。</li><li>選修科目：至少需修畢24學分，本系選修至少18學分；選修大學部課程，所上只承認本系大四課程二門。</li><li>外籍生除必修書報討論（0學分，2學期）及論文外，必須修滿經指導教授認可之選修課程24學分；選修大學部課程，所上只承認本系大四課程二門。</li><li>系統選課前須填寫指導教授「選課同意表」，並經指導教授同意後使可選課，若擅自更改科目，爾後系上不承認該學分時不得有異議。</li><li>其他相關規定請參閱網址http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/各項法規/課業/研究所(碩士班)/碩士班修業辦法。<ol><li>Minimum credits for graduation: 30 credits (include 6 credits for Thesis)</li><li>The Required Courses: Seminar (0 credit) is finished within two years.</li><li>At least take 24 credits for Elective Courses. 18 credits out of 24 credits are related to Mechanical Engineering courses. For elective courses of undergraduate school, the ME department only admits two courses of senior year.</li><li>Foreign students take not only “Seminar ME503 (0 credit, two semesters) and Thesis”, but also elective courses with 24 credits by your advisor approved. For elective courses of undergraduate school, the ME department only admits two courses of senior year.</li><li>Before you click courses on the portal system, you should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and then be approved by the advisor. To avoid credits dispute, don’t change it directly by yourself.</li><li>Others rules refer to http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10141.</li></ol></li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

colspan="4"><ol><li>最低畢業學分數：30學分（包含6學分論文）。</li><li>必修科目：書報討論（0學分）需於兩年內修完。</li><li>選修科目：至少需修畢24學分，本系選修至少18學分；選修大學部課程，所上只承認本系大四課程二門。</li><li>外籍生除必修書報討論（0學分，2學期）及論文外，必須修滿經指導教授認可之選修課程24學分；選修大學部課程，所上只承認本系大四課程二門。外籍生得加選一科3學分研究所課程抵免二學期「書報討論」。</li><li>系統選課前須填寫指導教授「選課同意表」，並經指導教授同意後使可選課，若擅自更改科目，爾後系上不承認該學分時不得有異議。</li><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</li><li>其他相關規定請參閱網址http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/各項法規/課業/研究所(碩士班)/碩士班修業辦法。<ol><li>Minimum credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis).</li><li>The required course is ME503 Seminar (0 credit for two semesters) which has to be completed within two years.</li><li>At least take 24 credits for elective courses. 18 credits out of the 24 credits are related to the mechanical engineering courses. For elective courses, the ME department only admits two courses from the fourth year of undergraduate program.</li><li>Foreign students take not only ME503 Seminar (0 credit for two semesters) and thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. For elective courses, the ME department only admits two courses from the fourth year of undergraduate program. Foreign students can take one additional graduate three-credit course in lieu of ME503 Seminar for two semesters. </li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10141</a>.</li></ol></li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

AA-CP-04-CF06 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis).</li><li>The required course is ME503 Seminar (0 credit for two semesters) which has to be completed within two years.</li><li>At least take 24 credits for elective courses. 18 credits out of the 24 credits are related to the mechanical engineering courses. For elective courses, the ME department only admits two courses from the fourth year of undergraduate program.</li><li>Foreign students take not only ME503 Seminar (0 credit for two semesters) and thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. For elective courses, the ME department only admits two courses from the fourth year of undergraduate program. Foreign students can take one additional graduate three-credit course in lieu of ME503 Seminar for two semesters. </li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10141</a>.</li></ol></li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

AA-CP-04-CF06 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis).</li><li>The required course is ME503 Seminar (0 credit for two semesters) which has to be completed within two years.</li><li>At least take 24 credits for elective courses. 18 credits out of the 24 credits are related to the mechanical engineering courses. For elective courses, the ME department only admits two courses from the fourth year of undergraduate program.</li><li>Foreign students take not only ME503 Seminar (0 credit for two semesters) and thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. For elective courses, the ME department only admits two courses from the fourth year of undergraduate program. Foreign students can take one additional graduate three-credit course in lieu of ME503 Seminar for two semesters. </li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10141</a>.</li></ol></li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

Algebra</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>ME583</p></td><td><p>推進系統概論與應用</p></td><td><p>Rocket Propulsion System</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>ME590</p></td><td><p>醫學工程原理與應用</p></td><td><p>Principle and Applications of Biomedical Engineering</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>ME610</p></td><td><p>創新產品設計</p></td><td><p>Innovative Product Design</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>ME611</p></td><td><p>創新產品開發實務</p></td><td><p>Innovative Product Development Practice</p></td><td><p>3</p></td></tr><tr><td><p>備註</p><p>Remarks</p></td><td colspan="4"><ol><li>最低畢業學分數：30學分（包含6學分論文）。</li><li>必修科目：書報討論（0學分）需於兩年內修完。</li><li>選修科目：至少需修畢24學分，本系選修至少18學分；選修大學部課程，所上只承認本系大四課程二門。</li><li>外籍生除必修書報討論（0學分，2學期）及論文外，必須修滿經指導教授認可之選修課程24學分；選修大學部課程，所上只承認本系大四課程二門。外籍生得加選一科3學分研究所課程抵免二學期「書報討論」。</li><li>系統選課前須填寫指導教授「選課同意表」，並經指導教授同意後使可選課，若擅自更改科目，爾後系上不承認該學分時不得有異議。</li><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</li><li>其他相關規定請參閱網址http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/學生事務/課程與修業/研究所(碩士班)/碩士班修業辦法。<ol><li>Minimum credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis).</li><li>The required course is ME503 Seminar (0 credit for two semesters) which has to be completed within two years.</li><li>At least take 24 credits for elective courses. 18 credits out of the 24 credits are related to the mechanical engineering courses. For elective courses, the ME department only admits two courses from the fourth year of undergraduate program.</li><li>Foreign students take not only ME503 Seminar (0 credit for two semesters) and thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. For elective courses, the ME department only admits two courses from the fourth year of undergraduate program. Foreign students can take one additional graduate three-credit course in lieu of ME503 Seminar for two semesters. </li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10141</a>.</li></ol></li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

AA-CP-04-CF06 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis).</li><li>The required course is ME503 Seminar (0 credit for two semesters) which has to be completed within two years.</li><li>At least take 24 credits for elective courses. 18 credits out of the 24 credits are related to the mechanical engineering courses. For elective courses, the ME department only admits two courses from the fourth year of undergraduate program.</li><li>Foreign students take not only thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. </li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10141</a>.</li></ol></li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis).</li><li>The required course is ME503 Seminar (0 credit for two semesters) which has to be completed within two years.</li><li>At least take 24 credits for elective courses. 18 credits out of the 24 credits are related to the mechanical engineering courses. For elective courses, the ME department only admits two courses from the fourth year of undergraduate program.</li><li>Foreign students take not only thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. </li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10141</a>.</li></ol></li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

AA-CP-04-CF06 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis).</li><li>At least take 24 credits for elective courses. 18 credits out of the 24 credits are related to the mechanical engineering courses. </li><li>Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form. Credits taken across academic systems are allowed to be counted as graduation credits, up to a maximum of 6 credits.</li><li>Foreign students take not only thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. </li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/</a> .</li></ol></li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

colspan="5"><ol><li>最低畢業學分數：30學分（包含6學分論文）。</li><li>選修科目：至少需修畢研究所課程24學分，本表選修課程至少18學分。</li><li>碩士班/碩專班跨學制修課之學分數准予納入畢業學分。欲跨學制修課之學生，須填寫「元智大學課程跨學制申請表」，跨學制修課之學分數准予納入畢業學分至多6學分。</li><li>外籍生(不含僑生及陸生)除論文外，必須修滿經指導教授認可之選修課程24學分（限研究所課程）。</li><li>系統選課前須填寫指導教授「選課同意表」，並經指導教授同意後使可選課，若擅自更改科目，爾後系上不承認該學分時不得有異議。</li><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</li><li>其他相關規定請參閱網址http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/學生事務/修業辦法。<ol><li>Minimum credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis).</li><li>At least take 24 credits for elective courses. 18 credits out of the 24 credits are related to the mechanical engineering courses. </li><li>Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form. Credits taken across academic systems are  allowed to be counted as graduation credits, up to a maximum of 6 credits.</li><li>Foreign students take not only thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. </li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/</a> .</li></ol></li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.3版)／113.12.16修訂

AA-CP-04-CF06 (1.3版)／113.12.16修訂

colspan="4"><ol><li>最低畢業學分數：36學分，除必修科目外，應符合以下其中之一項規定，始得畢業：<ol><li>撰寫技術性論文（3學分）及修畢選修課程33學分（其中本所課程至少21學分）。</li><li>撰寫學術性論文（12學分）及修畢選修課程24學分（其中本所課程至少12學分）。</li></ol></li><li>必修科目：書報討論（0學分，2學期）需於畢業前修完。</li><li>系統選課前須填寫指導教授「選課同意表」，並經指導教授同意後使可選課，若擅自更改科目，爾後系上不承認該學分時不得有異議。</li><li>選修本系大四課程，所上只承認二門課（6學分）。</li><li>其他相關規定請參閱網址http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/各項法規/課業/研究所(碩士班)/ 碩士在職專班修業辦法。<ol><li>Minimum credits for graduation: 36 credits.</li></ol></li></ol><p>Please choose one out of the both rules:</p><p>(1) Technical Thesis: 33 courses credits within 21 credits are related to Mechanical Engineering courses. 3 credits for Thesis.</p><p>(2) Academic Thesis: 24 courses credits within 12 credits are related to Mechanical Engineering courses. 12 credits for Thesis.</p><ul><li><ol><li>The Required Courses: Seminar ME503 (0 credit, two semesters) is finished within two years.</li><li>Before you click courses on portal system, you should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and then be approved by your advisor. To avoid credits dispute, don’t change it directly by yourself.</li><li>The ME department only admits two courses for senior year of undergraduate. (six credits).</li><li>Others rules refer to http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10141.</li></ol></li></ul></td></tr></tbody></table>

碩士在職專班修業辦法。</li><li>Please choose one of two rules for graduation:<ol><li>Technical Thesis: </li></ol></li></ol><p>Minimum credits for graduation: 36 credits, including 33 credits from required and elective courses ( at least 21 credits must relate to Mechanical Engineering Master degree courses).</p><ul><li><ol><li>Academic Thesis: </li></ol></li></ul><p>Minimum credits for graduation: 30 credits, including 24 credits from required and elective courses ( at least 15 credits must relate to Mechanical Engineering Master degree courses).</p><ol><li>The Mechanical Engineering department admits only two fourth year undergraduate courses (i.e. 6 credits) for elective courses.</li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Others rules refer to http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10141.</li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

AA-CP-04-CF06 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

碩士在職專班修業辦法。</li><li>Please choose one of two rules for graduation:<ol><li>Technical Thesis: </li></ol></li></ol><p>Minimum credits for graduation: 36 credits, including 33 credits from required and elective courses ( at least 21 credits must relate to Mechanical Engineering Master degree courses).</p><ul><li><ol><li>Academic Thesis: </li></ol></li></ul><p>Minimum credits for graduation: 30 credits, including 24 credits from required and elective courses ( at least 15 credits must relate to Mechanical Engineering Master degree courses).</p><ol><li>The Mechanical Engineering department admits only two fourth year undergraduate courses (i.e. 6 credits) for elective courses.</li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Others rules refer to http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10141.</li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Others rules refer to http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/.</li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

AA-CP-04-CF03 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

choose one of two rules for graduation:<ol><li>Technical Thesis: </li></ol></li></ol><p>Minimum credits for graduation: 36 credits, including 33 credits from required and elective courses ( at least 21 credits must relate to Mechanical Engineering Master degree courses).</p><ul><li><ol><li>Academic Thesis: </li></ol></li></ul><p>Minimum credits for graduation: 30 credits, including 24 credits from required and elective courses ( at least 15 credits must relate to Mechanical Engineering Master degree courses).</p><ol><li>The Mechanical Engineering department admits only two fourth year undergraduate courses (i.e. 6 credits) for elective courses.</li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Others rules refer to http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/.</li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

choose one of two rules for graduation:<ol><li>Technical Thesis: </li></ol></li></ol><p>Minimum credits for graduation: 36 credits, including 33 credits from required and elective courses (at least 21 credits must relate to Mechanical Engineering Master degree courses).</p><ul><li><ol><li>Academic Thesis: </li></ol></li></ul><p>Minimum credits for graduation: 30 credits, including 24 credits from required and elective courses (at least 15 credits must relate to Mechanical Engineering Master degree courses).</p><ol><li>The Mechanical Engineering department admits only two fourth year undergraduate courses (i.e. 6 credits) for elective courses.</li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Others rules refer to http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/.</li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

choose one of two rules for graduation:<ol><li>Technical Thesis: </li></ol></li></ol><p>Minimum credits for graduation: 36 credits, including 33 credits from required and elective courses (at least 21 credits must relate to Mechanical Engineering Master degree courses).</p><ul><li><ol><li>Academic Thesis: </li></ol></li></ul><p>Minimum credits for graduation: 30 credits, including 24 credits from required and elective courses (at least 15 credits must relate to Mechanical Engineering Master degree courses).</p><ol><li>The Mechanical Engineering department admits only two fourth year undergraduate courses (i.e. 6 credits) for elective courses.</li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Others rules refer to http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/.</li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 3 credits for thesis).</li><li>At least take 27 credits for elective courses. 21 credits out of the 27 credits are related to the mechanical engineering courses. </li><li>Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form. Credits taken across academic systems are    allowed to be counted as graduation credits, up to a maximum of 6 credits.</li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Others rules refer to http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/.</li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis). Please take 12 credits from the above list, and the rest of credits are approved by the advisor. You can register graduate courses from ME department and other departments.</li><li>Foreign students take not only thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. </li><li>PhD students taking In-service graduate courses are not allowed to be counted as graduation credits. Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form.</li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/.</a> </li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

colspan="4"><ol><li>最低畢業學分數：30學分（包含3學分技術論文）。</li><li>選修科目：至少需修畢研究所課程27學分，本表選修課程至少21學分。</li><li>碩士班/碩專班跨學制修課之學分數准予納入畢業學分。欲跨學制修課之學生，須填寫「元智大學課程跨學制申請表」，跨學制修課之學分數准予納入畢業學分至多6學分。</li><li>系統選課前須填寫指導教授「選課同意表」，並經指導教授同意後使可選課，若擅自更改科目，爾後系上不承認該學分時不得有異議。</li><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</li><li>其他相關規定請參閱網址http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/學生事務/修業辦法。</li><li>Minimum credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 3 credits for thesis).</li><li>At least take 27 credits for elective courses. 21 credits out of the 27 credits are related to the mechanical engineering courses. </li><li>Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form. Credits taken across academic systems are    allowed to be counted as graduation credits, up to a maximum of 6 credits.</li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete <strong>Academic Research Ethics Education Course</strong> by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Others rules refer to http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/.</li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

博士班修業辦法。</li><li>Minimum credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis).</li></ol><p>Please take 12 credits out of 30 credits from the above list, and the rest of credits are approved by the advisor. You can register graduate courses from ME department and other departments.</p><ol><li>The required courses are “One Out of Four Courses” and ME503 Seminar (0 credit for two semesters) which have to be completed before graduation.</li><li>Foreign students take not only ME503 Seminar (0 credit for two semesters) and thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. For elective courses, the ME department only admits two courses from the fourth year of undergraduate program. Foreign students can take one additional graduate three-credit course in lieu of ME503 Seminar for two semesters. </li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10142</a></li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

AA-CP-04-CF04 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

AA-CP-04-CF07 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂
```

The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10142</a></li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

Please take 12 credits from the above list, and the rest of credits are approved by the advisor. You can register graduate courses from ME department and other departments.</li><li>Foreign students take not only thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. </li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10142</a></li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

You can register graduate courses from ME department and other departments.</li><li>Foreign students take not only thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. </li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10142</a></li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

元智大學機械工程學系博士班必選修科目表

（109學年度入學新生適用）

**List of Required and Elective Courses for Doctorate Degree of the Department of Mechanical Engineering of Yuan Ze University**

**（Applicable to Students Admitted for Academic year of 2020-2021）**

109.05.06 一○八學年度第六次教務會議通過

Passed by the 6th Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2019, on May 06, 2020

109.11.11 一○九學年度第二次教務會議修訂通過

Amended by the 2nd Academic Affairs Meeting, Academic Year 2020, on November 11, 2020

博士班修業辦法。</li><li>Minimum credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis and 3 credits for required courses). Please take 12 credits from the above list, and the rest of credits are approved by the advisor. You can register graduate courses from ME department and other departments.</li><li>Foreign students take not only thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. </li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10142</a></li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

AA-CP-04-CF07 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis and 3 credits for required courses). Please take 12 credits from the above list, and the rest of credits are approved by the advisor. You can register graduate courses from ME department and other departments.</li><li>Foreign students take not only thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. </li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/menu/index/id/10142</a></li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

colspan="4"><ol><li>最低畢業學分數：30學分。除論文(6學分)及四選一必修(3學分)外，其中至少需修畢列於本表12學分之選修課程，其餘學分數經指導教授同意後，可修習外所（限研究所）課程。</li><li>外籍生除論文外，必須修滿經指導教授認可之選修課程24學分（限研究所）。</li><li>系統選課前須填寫指導教授「選課同意表」，並經指導教授同意後使可選課，若擅自更改科目，爾後系上不承認該學分時不得有異議。</li><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</li><li>相關規定請參閱網址http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/學生事務/修業辦法。</li><li>Minimum credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis and 3 credits for required courses). Please take 12 credits from the above list, and the rest of credits are approved by the advisor. You can register graduate courses from ME department and other departments.</li><li>Foreign students take not only thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. </li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/.</a> </li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

AA-CP-04-CF04 (1.2版)／101.11.15修訂

AA-CP-04-CF07 (1.2版)／101.11.15修

colspan="4"><ol><li>最低畢業學分數：30學分。除論文(6學分)外，其中至少需修畢列於本表12學分之選修課程，其餘學分數經指導教授同意後，可修習外所（限研究所）課程。</li><li>外籍生除論文外，必須修滿經指導教授認可之選修課程24學分（限研究所）。</li><li>博士班學生選修碩士在職專班之課程，不列入畢業學分，須填寫「元智大學課程跨學制申請表」。</li><li>系統選課前須填寫指導教授「選課同意表」，並經指導教授同意後使可選課，若擅自更改科目，爾後系上不承認該學分時不得有異議。</li><li>入學研究生須依本校學術研究倫理教育課程實施要點規定，於入學第一學期結束前完成學術研究倫理教育課程，最遲須於申請學位口試前補修完成，未完成本課程，不得申請學位口試。</li><li>相關規定請參閱網址http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/學生事務/修業辦法。</li><li>Minimum credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis). Please take 12 credits from the above list, and the rest of credits are approved by the advisor. You can register graduate courses from ME department and other departments.</li><li>Foreign students take not only thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. </li><li>PhD students taking In-service graduate courses are not allowed to be counted as graduation credits. Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form.</li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/.</a> </li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

AA-CP-04-CF04 (1.3版)／113.12.16修訂

AA-CP-04-CF07 (1.3版)／113.12.16修訂
```

credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis). Please take 12 credits from the above list, and the rest of credits are approved by the advisor. You can register graduate courses from ME department and other departments.</li><li>Foreign students take not only thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. </li><li>PhD students taking In-service graduate courses are not allowed to be counted as graduation credits. Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form.</li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/.</a> </li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>

credits for graduation are 30 credits (including 6 credits for thesis). Please take 12 credits from the above list, and the rest of credits are approved by the advisor. You can register graduate courses from ME department and other departments.</li><li>Foreign students take not only thesis, but also elective courses with 24 credits approved by your advisor. </li><li>PhD students taking In-service graduate courses are not allowed to be counted as graduation credits. Students who would like to apply for Cross-System Courses need to fill in the "Application for Cross-System Courses" form.</li><li>All graduate students should fill out “Advisor Approval Courses Form” and be approved by the advisor before register any courses on the portal system. The form cannot be changed by yourself to avoid disputes.</li><li>Based on the regulations of Yuan Ze University Academic Research Ethics Education Course Implementation Highlights, all graduate students should complete Academic Research Ethics Education Course by the end of first semester. The deadline for the course completion has to be the date before the application of thesis oral defense. "No Course and No Defense."</li><li>Other rules refer to <a>http://www.mech.yzu.edu.tw/.</a> </li></ol></td></tr></tbody></table>
